10.2(1): khams su/ bag chags sreg pa'i me ri sna tshogs 'bar/ las ngan log sreg zad 
10.3(1): cing stong par byed/ ye shes rol pa'i me ri mkha' la 'bar/ rtogs pa dbyings kyi 
10.4(1): me ri sems la 'bar/ gzi byin sprul pa'i me ri phyag rgyar 'bar/ thugs rje kun 
10.5(1): 'byung me ri ma rtogs bdud la 'bar/ khro bo dbal gyi me ri log 'dren 'byung po'i

10.12(1): kyus nyon mongs 'dzin/ zhags pas mtho ris gnas su 'dren/ tho bas las dang 
10.13(1): bag chags brdung / mda' gzhus rig pa'i ye shes bskyed/ e nyid mi 'gyur bon

122.17(1): yid spro sems gsal dang / bsgom pa'i don gsal ngang gnas pa/ phugs kyi drod 
122.18(1): ste rteng mi 'cha'/ rgod nas 'khor ba sgyid lug bya/ skyon yon gnyis med mnyam

123.1(1): shu gsum pa'o// //
123.2(1): 7 ston pa'i sgron mas bka' stsal pa/ bon nyid rang bzhin rnam par dag /yon 
123.3(1): tan thams cad 'byung ba'i klong / ma 'gag rgyan gyi 'od zer 'phro/ sku lnga lhun gyis 
123.4(1): grub pa'i ngang / ma rig ma rtogs 'khrul pa yi/ dug lnga'i bag chags mthu rtas 
123.5(1): pas/ zag bcas skyon gyi phung por grub/ rgyu bzhi gzugs kyi phung po la/ nang gi 
123.6(1): sdug bsngal rnam pa bzhi/ dang por skye ba'i sdug bsngal dang / 'gyu ba rgas pa'i sdug 
123.7(1): bsngal dang / mi rtag 'chi ba'i sdug bsngal bzhi/ zo chu rgyun ma bzhin du 'byung / phyi 
123.8(1): yi sdug bsngal rnam bzhi yis/ yod pa btsa' ba mi thub dang / med pa btsal du mi

123.10(1): las kyi ded dpon bzhin du 'byung / sdug bsngal phyi nang de dag kyang / dngos 
123.11(1): dang lhag pa'i sdug bsngal la/ de ba'i 'khrul pa'i sdug bsngal dang / dmyal ba tsha

123.13(1): sdug bsngal dang / mi la 'pho 'gyur sdug bsngal dang / lha men 'thab rtsod sdug 
123.14(1): bsngal dang / lha la pham ltung sdug bsngal dang / sdug bsngal bye brag bsam 'das pa/
123.15(1): dper na chu gzhung gnyer ma ltar/ ma rig 'khrul pa'i mtsho las byung / sdug bsngal 
123.16(1): 'khor ba rgyun gcod phyir/ bon nyid mi g.yo bde ba che/ rnam par mi rtog thams cad 
123.17(1): mkhyen/ dang po rgyu zhes ma skyes med/ rgas rgud med pa'i ye shes bde/ 'gal ba 
123.18(1): med pa'i rang byung bde/ tha ma rkyen gyi mi 'gag med/ bde ba chen po'i ngang gnas 
123.19(1): pa/ nang gi sdug bsngal rang dag sangs/ snang ba sgyu ma yin pas chags sems med/
123.20(1): ma g.yos bde ba chen po la/ ngang la gnas shing gsal rtogs pa/ phyi'i sdug bsngal 
123.21(1): rang dag sangs/ brtsal med bde chen lhun la rdzogs/ rnam par mi rtog rtsol dang 
124.1(1): bral/ ye nas bde chen bon gyi sku/ che ba'i yon tan longs spyod rdzogs/ 'gro 'dul 
124.2(1): thugs rje cir yang sprul/ bye brag ngo bo nyid du grub/ ma spangs lhun grub 'bras bu

124.10(1): rgyud las/ sdug bsngal rgyun gcod bstan pa'i le'u ste nyi shu bzhi pa'o// //
124.11(1): 7 ston pa'i sgron mas bka' stsal pa/ 'gyur med g.yung drung bon gyi dbyings/

124.21(1): bcud phyi nang thams cad kun/ rnam gsum yig 'bru phyag mtshan dang / yongs

432.14(1): lhun gyis 'grub pa dang / 'brel thogs kyi sbyin pa'i bdag po dang las gzhi 'di'i byed 
432.15(1): po kun tshe bsod dbang khams gong nas gong du mtho ste myur du sku gsum rdzogs pa'i 
432.16(1): sangs rgyas kyi go 'phang thob pa dang / zhang bod rig gzhung rnams mi nyams gong nas 
432.17(1): gong du 'phel te 'dzam gling tha gru yongs kyi snod bcud rgud pa gso zhing phan bde'i 
432.18(1): gsos su khyab pa dang / yangs pa'i rgyal khams kun du nad mug 'khrug rtsod dang rang 
432.19(1): byung 'byung ba'i 'jigs pa rnams rmeng med du zhi nas bde legs phun tshogs skyid kyi nyi
